Here are the rosters as of Sunday, June 18, 2006.  Please review and 
make sure that the information is accurate.  Refer corrections to 
Anthony Camargo at ajcam@sbcglobal.net.  Changes must be made by 
Monday, June 19, 2006 to show up correctly in the PAJOs program.  
Any corrections, changes, additions, deletions, etc. made after 
Monday will not be reflected.  Changes can be made up until Tuesday, 
which will not be reflected in the program, but will be changed 
in time for the actual track meet.
